{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=;
    Time=;
    Version List=4PS9.00.SMART.TESTEN;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    CaptionML=ENU=Check Item Usage;
    OnInitReport=BEGIN

                   FooterInfo := Text001; //A = ontbrekend artikel; B = artikel geblokkeerd; C = onjuiste eenheid;
                 END;

    OnPreReport=BEGIN

                  IF ExportToExcel THEN BEGIN
                    CREATE(xlApp,FALSE,TRUE);
                    xlBook := xlApp.Workbooks.Add;
                    xlSheet := xlApp.Sheets.Add;
                    xlApp.DisplayAlerts := FALSE;
                    xlSheet.Name := FORMAT('Artikel_gegevens');
                    xlSheet.Select;
                    RowNo := 4;
                    xlSheet.Range( 'A1:C1').Merge;
                    xlSheet.Range( 'A1' ).Value := 'Artikel gegevens';
                    xlSheet.Range( 'A2' ).Value := FORMAT(TODAY);

                    xlSheet.Range( 'A4' ).Value := 'Type';
                    xlSheet.Range( 'A4' ).ColumnWidth := 8.43;
                    xlSheet.Range( 'B4' ).Value := 'Recipe Group';
                    xlSheet.Range( 'B4' ).ColumnWidth := 8.43;
                    xlSheet.Range( 'C4' ).Value := 'Nr.';
                    xlSheet.Range( 'C4' ).ColumnWidth := 15.71;
                    xlSheet.Range( 'D4' ).Value := 'Omschrijving';
                    xlSheet.Range( 'D4' ).ColumnWidth := 34.43;
                    xlSheet.Range( 'E4' ).Value := 'Soort';
                    xlSheet.Range( 'E4' ).ColumnWidth := 8.43;
                    xlSheet.Range( 'F4' ).Value := 'Artikel nr.';
                    xlSheet.Range( 'F4' ).ColumnWidth := 15.43;
                    xlSheet.Range( 'G4' ).Value := 'Fabr. / Lev.';
                    xlSheet.Range( 'G4' ).ColumnWidth := 16.29;
                    xlSheet.Range( 'H4' ).Value := 'FoutCode';
                    xlSheet.Range( 'H4' ).ColumnWidth := 18.29;
                    xlSheet.Range('A1:H4').Font.Bold := TRUE;
                  END;
                END;

    OnPostReport=BEGIN

                   IF ExportToExcel THEN BEGIN
                     xlApp.Range('A5:H5').Select;
                     xlApp.ActiveWindow.FreezePanes := TRUE;
                     xlSheet.Range('A4:H4').AutoFilter;
                     xlApp.Visible := TRUE;
                     xlApp.UserControl := TRUE;
                     ERROR('');
                   END;
                 END;

  }

    { 1100525007;0;DataItem;                 ;
               DataItemTable=Table99;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Item No.,Variant Code,Vendor No.);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN

                               IF AlternItemBl = FALSE THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  lvItem@1100525000 : Record 27;
                                BEGIN

                                  ItemBlocked := FALSE;
                                  ItemFound := TRUE;
                                  InvalidUnit := FALSE;
                                  ErrorCode := '';

                                  IF "Vendor Item No." <>'' THEN BEGIN
                                    IF NOT TradeItemRec.GET("Vendor (Trade Item)","Item Vendor"."Vendor Item No.") THEN
                                      ItemFound := FALSE
                                    ELSE
                                      IF TradeItemRec.Expired THEN
                                        ItemBlocked := TRUE;
                                  END;
                                  IF NOT CheckItemMeasure THEN
                                    InvalidUnit := TRUE;

                                  IF ItemFound = FALSE THEN
                                    ErrorCode := 'A'
                                  ELSE
                                    IF ItemBlocked = TRUE THEN
                                      ErrorCode := 'B'
                                    ELSE
                                      ErrorCode := 'C';
                                  IF ErrorCode = '' THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  //FROM SECTIONS

                                  lvItem.GET("Item No.");
                                  DescriptionTxt := lvItem.Description;
                                END;
                                 }

      xlSheet@1100525006 : Automation "{00020813-0000-0000-C000-000000000046} 1.5:{00020820-0000-0000-C000-000000000046}:Unknown Automation Server.Worksheet";
      xlSheets@1100525005 : Automation "{00020813-0000-0000-C000-000000000046} 1.6:{000208B1-0000-0000-C000-000000000046}:Unknown Automation Server.Worksheets";
      xlRange@1100525004 : Automation "{00020813-0000-0000-C000-000000000046} 1.6:{00020846-0000-0000-C000-000000000046}:Unknown Automation Server.Range";

      CellCde@1100525002 : ARRAY [100] OF Code[20];

    PROCEDURE CheckItem@1(lvItem@1210190000 : Code[20];lvBasicItem@1210190001 : Code[20];lvTradeItem@1210190002 : Code[20];lvManufacturer@1210190004 : Code[20];lvVendor@1210190005 : Code[20];lvDesc@1210190006 : Text[100];lvUnit@1100485000 : Code[10]);
    VAR
      ItemUnitRec@1100485001 : Record 5404;
    BEGIN
      ItemFound := TRUE;
      ItemBlocked := FALSE;
      InvalidUnit := FALSE;
      ItemCode := '';
      MV := '';
      ErrorCode := '';
      IF lvTradeItem <> '' THEN BEGIN
        ItemCode := lvTradeItem;
        MV := lvVendor;
        ItemType := COPYSTR(TradeItemRec.TABLECAPTION, 1,1);
        IF NOT TradeItemRec.GET(lvVendor, lvTradeItem) THEN
          ItemFound := FALSE
        ELSE
          ItemBlocked := TradeItemRec.Expired;
        IF ((lvUnit <> UPPERCASE(TradeItemRec."Application Unit")) AND
            (lvUnit <> UPPERCASE(TradeItemRec."Packaging Unit"))) OR
           (lvUnit = '') THEN InvalidUnit := TRUE;
      END ELSE BEGIN
        IF lvBasicItem <> '' THEN BEGIN
          ItemCode := lvBasicItem;
          MV := lvManufacturer;
          ItemType := COPYSTR(BasicItemRec.TABLECAPTION, 1,1);
          IF NOT BasicItemRec.GET(lvManufacturer, lvBasicItem) THEN
            ItemFound := FALSE
          ELSE
            ItemBlocked := BasicItemRec.Expired;
          IF ((lvUnit <> UPPERCASE(BasicItemRec."Application Unit")) AND
              (lvUnit <> UPPERCASE(BasicItemRec."Packaging Unit"))) OR
             (lvUnit = '') THEN InvalidUnit := TRUE;
        END ELSE BEGIN
          IF lvItem <> '' THEN BEGIN
            ItemCode := lvItem;
            MV := '';
            ItemType := COPYSTR(ItemRec.TABLECAPTION, 1,1);
            IF NOT ItemRec.GET(lvItem) THEN
              ItemFound := FALSE
            ELSE
              ItemBlocked := ItemRec.Blocked;
            IF NOT ItemUnitRec.GET(lvItem, lvUnit) THEN
              InvalidUnit := TRUE;
          END;
        END;
      END;

      //db.sn, 20-08-09: M14331
      IF (ItemFound = TRUE) AND (ItemBlocked = FALSE) AND (InvalidUnit = FALSE) THEN BEGIN
        IF (lvBasicItem + lvTradeItem <> '') AND (lvItem <> '') THEN BEGIN
          ItemCode := lvItem;
          MV := '';
          ItemType := COPYSTR(ItemRec.TABLECAPTION, 1,1);
          IF NOT ItemRec.GET(lvItem) THEN
            ItemFound := FALSE
          ELSE
            ItemBlocked := ItemRec.Blocked;
          IF NOT ItemUnitRec.GET(lvItem, lvUnit) THEN
            InvalidUnit := TRUE;
        END;
      END;
      //db.en, 20-08-09: M14331

      IF ItemFound = FALSE THEN
        ErrorCode := 'A'
      ELSE
        IF ItemBlocked = TRUE THEN
          ErrorCode := 'B'
        ELSE
          IF InvalidUnit = TRUE THEN
            ErrorCode := 'C';

      IF ErrorCode = '' THEN CurrReport.SKIP;
    END;

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
